Top 32 Decklists
================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on June 28, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/hero/wizardslogo_thumb.jpg)
By Jacob Van Lunen and Marc Calderaro











We all know how much you guys like decklists. Here are the rest of the Top 32 players who just missed out on those 1 through 8 slots.
